## v1.3.3-pre.11 (prerelease)

Changes since v1.3.3-pre.10:

- Migrate ktsu.io to ktsu namespace ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Add LICENSE template ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Add automation scripts for metadata generation and project management ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Make WasOpen public ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Renamed metadata files ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update FilesystemBrowser usage of BeginChild and BeginTable ([@Damon3000s](https://github.com/Damon3000s))
- Fix wrong namespace ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Replace LICENSE file with LICENSE.md and update copyright information ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Initial commit ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update project SDK references to ktsu.Sdk.Lib and ktsu.Sdk.App version 1.8.0 in ImGuiPopups and ImGuiPopupsDemo projects. ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update ImGuiStyler and ImGuiApp package references to latest alpha versions ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Remove icon to fix LFS ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Remove unused package reference ([@Damon3000s](https://github.com/Damon3000s))
- Update packages ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update package references and fix namespace in ImGuiPopupsDemo ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Add support for wrapped messages and custom popup sizes ([@Damon3000s](https://github.com/Damon3000s))
- Migrate ktsu.io to ktsu namespace ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Addressing PR feedback ([@Damon3000s](https://github.com/Damon3000s))
- Update packages ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Remove Directory.Build.props and Directory.Build.targets files, and delete associated scripts for metadata and version management. Update ImGuiPopups and related files to include copyright information and refactor variable declarations for consistency. ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update ImGui.NET ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update editorconfig and fix build errors ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update StrongPaths package reference to version 1.1.31 in ImGuiPopups.csproj ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Readd icon ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Update package references to latest versions in ImGuiPopups.csproj ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
- Ensure the BeginListBox return value is checked before calling EndListBox ([@matt-edmondson](https://github.com/matt-edmondson))
